    SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[AssignedLocationId], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsLoginEnabled], [u].[LastLoginAt], [u].[LastName], [u].[Phone], [u].[Role]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    WHERE [u].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ORDER BY [u].[FirstName]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Locations] AS [l] ON [t].[AssignedLocationId] = [l].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[FirstName]
